    [UserDetailId] bigint NOT NULL IDENTITY,
    [UserId] bigint NOT NULL,
    [FirstName] nvarchar(50) NOT NULL,
    [LastName] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [ProfileImage] varbinary(max) NULL,

    [Gender] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [CountryId] bigint NOT NULL,
    [StateId] bigint NOT NULL,
    [Region] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [Specialization] nvarchar(50) NOT NULL,
    [FollowersCount] int NULL,
    CONSTRAINT [PK_UserDetails] PRIMARY KEY ([UserDetailId]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_UserDetails_Countries_CountryId] FOREIGN KEY ([CountryId]) REFERENCES [Countries] ([CountryId]) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_UserDetails_States_StateId] FOREIGN KEY ([StateId]) REFERENCES [States] ([StateId]) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_UserDetails_Users_UserId] FOREIGN KEY ([UserId]) REFERENCES [Users] ([UserId]) ON DELETE CASCADE
